***hocus-pocus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a> (30511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Dates from the 17th century when used by jugglers and magicians as a nonsense magical incantation.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> Some believe it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a corruption of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> from the Roman Catholic liturgy of the Eucharist, <i><b>hoc est</b> enim <b>corpus</b> meum</i>, although this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> disputed. Accroding to Microsoft® Encarta® 2009, it <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a> from Pseudo-Latin <i>hax pax <a href = vnd.unilang:max.html>max</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>Deus</a> adimax</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>A phrase used as a magical incantation to bring about some change.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocuses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Trickery or nonsense.
<dl><dd><i>What <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> this?</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A conjurer.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A conjurer's trick.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocuses</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocusing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hocus-pocused</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cheat.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of L'Estrange to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hocus-pocus.html>hocus-pocus</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verouderde.html>verouderde</a> spelling of <a href = vnd.unilang:vorm.html>vorm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hocus.html>hocus</a> pocus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> vóór 2006</li></ol>
</body>

***hoe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> (52)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">huo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>how</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>forms a the parallel comparative</i>) the ... the

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Second <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a></i> can be replaced by <i><a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>; there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no difference between the two as they are purely a matter of preference, both are commonly used throughout the Dutch-speaking regions.
</p>

***hoed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a> (1758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hōdaz</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>Hut</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hood</i>.
</p>

</p>

***hoede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a> (5086)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoede</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoede.html>hoedes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heed, guard, alertness
<ul><li><b>1877</b>, H.A.M. Roelants, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>Geschiedenis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:consulaat.html>Consulaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keizerrijk.html>Keizerrijk</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a> (767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hōfaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱoph₂ós</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Huf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hoof</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hov</i>.

***hoepelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a> (39441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepel.html>hoepel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a> <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1683</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:steven.html>Steven</a> Blankaart, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Kartesiaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:academie.html>academie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofte.html>ofte</a>, institutie <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> medicyne</i>, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:johannes.html>Johannes</a> ten <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a>, page 205.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> datse <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> papsakken souden <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebieden.html>gebieden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:koten.html>koten</a>, knikkeren, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></b> amp;c. <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> tyd <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brengt.html>brengt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werden.html>werden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sy.html>sy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterk.html>sterk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> vrolyk.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">One should command the children, so that they do not become fat-asses, to play, to walk, play with dice, play with <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a>, <b>roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a></b> amp;c. in accordance with the time of year, this <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> them strong and happy.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:hula.html>hula</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoop.html>hoop</a> <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoelahoepen</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoelahoepelen</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go away, to get <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more commonly in derived expressions</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c., 18th c. in derivatives]</span>
<ul><li><b>1861</b>, François Haverschmidt (ed. René <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Slooten), <i><a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>Reis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> België <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:langs.html>langs</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:rijn.html>Rijn</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://dbnl.nl/tekst/have010reis02_01/colofon.php">DBNL</a> (2009), page 86.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoer.html>hoer</a> (1253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huora</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hōrǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***hoerenzoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a> (17496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hoerensone</i>, first attested as a gloss for <i>manzer</i>, i.e. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mamzer</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoer.html>hoer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whore, hooker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">interfix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">son</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whoreson</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hurensohn</i> and the <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">huorresoan</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> perhaps calqued from the Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzonen.html>hoerenzonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">whoreson</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">son of a <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">despicable <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> son of a whore, <span class="Latn" lang="en">whoreson</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">son of a usually female prostitute</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoerenzoon.html>hoerenzoon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***hoesten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a> (11806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*huoston</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwōstōną</i>, derived from the strong verb <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwōsaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷeh₂s-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoesten.html>hoesten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cough, push air from the lungs forcefully, as because of a cold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:suf.html>suffer</a> from a (disease which causes a) cough</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To clear one's throat, notably by emulating the above</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoestmiddel</span></li>

***hoeven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a> (1106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Cognates are attested much more sparsely, and <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, than those of the prefixed form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i>. It therefore appears that <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be necessary</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to, to have to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeft.html>hoeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoeken.html>zoeken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>have to</b> seek far.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeft.html>hoeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vragen.html>vragen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You only <b>need to</b> ask it.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoef.html>hoef</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I only <b>need</b> two (of them).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need to urinate or defecate, to need to go</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Whenever a finite form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></i> introduces a verb phrase, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> inserted before the first verb in the verb phrase.
</p>

***hof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a> (2509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hufą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoven.html>hoven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hof.html>hofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>) <span id="attentionseekingnl" class="attentionseeking" lang="nl" title="neuter and male, but needs sorting out which senses belong to which gender and where the difference arises etymologically"></span> 
</p>
<ol><li>(royal) court</li>
<li>court of law; short form of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gerechtshof.html>gerechtshof</a></b></li>
<li>court, yard</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:East Flanders">East</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Flanders" class="extiw" title="w:West Flanders">West Flanders</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> garden</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoho.html>hoho</a> (47222)</h1><br></body> 
***hoi.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a> (515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly a spontaneous alteration of the interjection <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a></i>. The use as a joyful exclamation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attested from the 16th century; use as an informal greeting appears only in the 20th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A greeting acknowledging someone’s arrival or presence, comparable to English <a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>hey</a>, hi
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>Hoi</a>,</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>?</i> — <a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, how's it going?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An exclamation of joy.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tante.html>tante</a> in Marokko <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a>, hiep <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoi.html>hoi</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have an aunt in Morocco and she's coming <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, yippee <b>yay</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoihoi</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***hok.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hok.html>hok</a> (8653)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hok.html>hok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hokken.html>hokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hokje.html>hokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A living shelter for domesticated animals such as a kennel, cage, <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a> or a <a href = vnd.unilang:pen.html>pen</a>.</li>
<li>A closet or small room.</li>
<li>A den; a small and often dark dwelling such as a <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>.</li></ol>

***hol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a> (4487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holen.html>holen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holletje.html>holletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hole, hollow, cavity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cargo hold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An <a href = vnd.unilang:anus.html>anus</a>, arsehole; both anatomical senses of butt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hol.html>hol</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zul.html>zul</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoonmaken.html>schoonmaken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> have to clean up your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b> yourself.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any other bodily cavity that resembles a hole</li>
<li>An artificial opening such as a slit</li>
<li>burrow (a hole or <a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>tunnel</a> dug by a small animal, like a rabbit, used as a dwelling)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unsanitary and/or unpleasant place; shithole</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hole</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gat.html>gat</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">opening</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aars.html>aars</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gat.html>gat</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reet.html>reet</a></span></li>

***holly.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a> (4601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holie</i>, a shortened variation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">holyn</i> (gt; English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hollen.html>hollen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">holm</i>), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">holeġn</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:holen.html>holen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a>; prince, protector</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulisaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butcher's broom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱol-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn, awn; a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of thorny plant; prickly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱel-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">holin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">hollin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">holyn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hulst.html>hulst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hulst.html>Hulst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">houx</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"<a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a>" lt; Germanic</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hylver</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">culmus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stalk, <a class="mention-gloss">ear of grain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:holly.html>holly</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hollies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various shrubs or (mostly) small trees, of the genus <i>Ilex</i>, either evergreen or deciduous, used as decoration especially at Christmas.</li>
<li>The wood from this tree.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a qualifier</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several unrelated plant species likened to <i>Ilex</i> because of their prickly, evergreen foliage and/or round, bright-red berries</li></ol>

***homeopathie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a> (75376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">homeopathy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">homéopathie</i>, etc.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Homeopathy</span>: a pseudomedical method invented by Hahnemann based on analogies between symptoms and <a href = vnd.unilang:remedies.html>remedies</a>, using extremely diluted <a href = vnd.unilang:doses.html>doses</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">homeopaat</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathisch.html>homeopathisch</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:homeopathie.html>homeopathie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alternatieve.html>alternatieve</a> geneeswijze <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorspronkelijk.html>oorspronkelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geformuleerd.html>geformuleerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Samuel Hahnemann <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gepubliceerd.html>gepubliceerd</a> in 1796

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">home</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">trainer</i>. A compound word coined by Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> using English component <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>. The compound does not exist in English, but does in German as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hometrainer.html>Hometrainer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stationary bicycle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***homo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a> (1728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homoseksueel.html>homoseksueel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a>'s</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homootje.html>homootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neutral<span class="ib-comma">,</span> not offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gay, homosexual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used as a general slur</span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:homo.html>homo</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a general, neutral and somewhat informal term for a homosexual person. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a slur by some, but the term, or its use in this way, can be considered offensive. Because the word itself <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not inherently offensive or vulgar, some people may take offense at the implication that homosexuality <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> something negative and shameful that could be used as a derogatory term. This depends, of course, on a particular person's attitude towards homosexuality. Compare similar usage of English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gay</i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
